msg:Before checking in, I called the hotel to confirm the arrival time and floor height requirements, and they were all met when I arrived. Communication was smooth. Check-in and check-out are very fast. Welcome fruits are given, four qualities are also available.
The room is very large and spacious, the bedding is relatively comfortable and clean, the bathtub is big enough for a comfortable soak, and a sink is a bit inconvenient. Marriott seems to like to have a sink for some reason. Yes, a hole was found on the floor towel. This is the first time it has been discovered in a five-star hotel. It needs to be carefully inspected and improved.
The location is very convenient. It is very close to the Ten Thousand Buddha Pagoda in Guzicheng. It only takes 15 hours and 20 minutes to walk there. However, if the scenery along the main road is too ordinary, you can take the bridge over Bayong Park. The scenery will be better.
When I checked in, I used my Marriott membership to get an extra breakfast, which is member-friendly! Everything you need for breakfast is available, so you can eat whatever you want. There are multiple coffee machines placed next to different dining tables and they are all equipped with takeaway cups, which is commendable! Very a**ospheric!
The overall feeling is good. At this price and quality, it is still recommended to stay!
